 developed Josephine of out a wave tropical strong which moved on August 31 off the coast African .

 became The wave quickly organized . declared Tropical Depression Ten located on September 2 while mi 170 ) km ( 270 to the southeast south @-@ of the Cape Verde Islands and was

 moved Josephine Over the days , several next in a direction northwest general west @-@ . reached intensity its peak on September 3 and early

 , On September 6 the combination of shear wind , air dry cooling and waters , caused to weaken into a depression tropical Josephine .

 Background = = = =

 signed the Treaty of San Ildefonso In 1796 , the Republic and French Spain after years of the Revolutionary Wars French three , .

 required to renounce its alliance with Britain Great and to declare on ally its former war subsequently Spain The terms secret of this treaty .

 meant this shift of allegiance political In the East Indies were with the threat of attack from the Philippines Spanish faced forces in the region British dominant the to the east that .

 dominated in 1796 Britain East Indies the controlling through the Ocean Indian the routes trade from the ports of Bombay and Calcutta Madras , , .
